Ù‚ÙÙ„ÙÙ‚","plural":"Ù‡ÙÙ…ÙÙˆÙ…","fem":"","present":"","source":"","collo_ar":"ÙŠÙØ­Ù’Ù…ÙÙ„Ù Ù‡ÙÙ…Ù‹Ù‘Ø§","collo_cn":"å¿ƒæ€€å¿§è™‘","sent_ar":"Ø£ÙØ²ÙØ§Ù„Ù Ø§Ù„Ù„Ù‡Ù Ù‡ÙÙ…ÙÙ‘ÙƒÙ.","sent_cn":"æ„¿ä¸»æ¶ˆé™¤ä½ çš„å¿§è™‘ã€‚"},{"id":67,"word":"Ø³ÙØ¹ÙØ§Ø¯ÙØ©","ipa":"[sa'Äda]","root":"Ø³Ø¹Ø¯","pos":"åè¯","def_cn":"å¹¸ç¦","def_ar":"ÙÙØ±ÙØ­ / Ø³ÙØ±ÙÙˆØ±","plural":"","fem":"","present":"","source":"","collo_ar":"Ø³ÙØ¹ÙØ§Ø¯ÙØ©Ù Ø§Ù„Ù’Ø£ÙØ³Ù’Ø±ÙØ©Ù","collo_cn":"å®¶åº­å¹¸ç¦","sent_ar":"Ø£ÙØªÙÙ…ÙÙ†ÙÙ‘Ù‰ Ù„ÙÙƒÙÙ…Ù Ø§Ù„Ø³ÙÙ‘Ø¹ÙØ§Ø¯ÙØ©Ù Ø§Ù„Ø¯ÙÙ‘Ø§Ø¦ÙÙ…ÙØ©Ù.","sent_cn":"æˆ‘ç¥ä½ ä»¬æ°¸è¿œå¹¸ç¦ã€‚"},{"id":68,"word":"ØªÙØ§Ù…Ù‘","ipa":"[tÄmm]","root":"ØªÙ…Ù…","pos":"å½¢å®¹è¯","def_cn":"å®Œå…¨çš„ï¼Œåœ†æ»¡çš„","def_ar":"ÙƒÙØ§Ù…ÙÙ„","plural":"","fem":"ØªÙØ§Ù…ÙÙ‘Ø©","present":"","source":"","collo_ar":"Ø´ÙÙÙØ§Ø¡ÙŒ ØªÙØ§Ù…ÙŒÙ‘","collo_cn":"å®Œå…¨åº·å¤","sent_ar":"Ù„ÙØ¯ÙÙŠÙÙ‘ Ø«ÙÙ‚ÙØ©ÙŒ ØªÙØ§Ù…ÙÙ‘Ø©ÙŒ Ø¨ÙÙƒÙ.","sent_cn":"æˆ‘å¯¹ä½ å®Œå…¨ä¿¡ä»»ã€‚"}]}];
let currentBookData = [], currentIndex = 0, score = 0, isAnswered = false, currentWordObj = null, currentMode = 'std', pointsPerWord = 0, canSpeak = false;
let matchPairs = [], selectedLeft = null, selectedRight = null, matchedCount = 0;

function stripTashkeel(str) { if(!str) return ""; return str.replace(/[\u064B-\u065F\u0670\u06D6-\u06ED]/g, ''); }
function createFuzzyRegex(word) { const bare = stripTashkeel(word); const pattern = bare.split('').join('[\\u064B-\\u065F\\u0670]*'); return new RegExp(pattern, 'g'); }
function checkTTS() { if ('speechSynthesis' in window) canSpeak = true; }
function shuffle(arr) { return arr.sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5); }

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => { checkTTS(); renderBookList(); });

function renderBookList() {
    const container = document.getElementById('bookListContainer'); container.innerHTML = "";
    LIBRARY.forEach((book, index) => {
        const div = document.createElement('div'); div.className = 'book-card';
        div.innerHTML = `<div><h3 style="margin:0">${book.title}</h3><p style="margin:5px 0 0 0;color:#888">${book.data.length} è¯</p></div><div style="color:#ccc">âœ</div>`;
        div.onclick = () => startBook(index); container.appendChild(div);
    });
}
function startBook(index) {
    currentBookData = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(LIBRARY[index].data)); shuffle(currentBookData);
    currentIndex = 0; score = 0; pointsPerWord = 100 / currentBookData.length;
    document.getElementById('homeView').classList.remove('active'); document.getElementById('quizView').classList.add('active');
    loadCard(0);
}
function goHome() { if(confirm("ç¡®å®šé€€å‡ºï¼Ÿè¿›åº¦ä¸ä¿å­˜")) { document.getElementById('quizView').classList.remove('active'); document.getElementById('homeView').classList.add('active'); closeSheet(); } }

function loadCard(index) {
    closeSheet();
    setTimeout(() => {
        isAnswered = false; currentWordObj = currentBookData[index];
        document.getElementById('progress-text').innerText = (index + 1) + " / " + currentBookData.length;
        document.getElementById('score-text').innerText = "å¾—åˆ†: " + Math.round(score);
        document.getElementById('btnShow').style.display = 'block'; 
        
        // æ ¸å¿ƒæ¦‚ç‡æ§åˆ¶
        const roll = Math.random();
        const hasSent = !!currentWordObj.sent_ar;
        
        // 0.00 - 0.15 : Match (15%)
        // 0.15 - 0.35 : Cloze (20%) [å¦‚æ— ä¾‹å¥åˆ™è½¬Std]
        // 0.35 - 0.60 : Rev (25%)
        // 0.60 - 1.00 : Std (40%)

        if (roll < 0.15) { 
            currentMode = 'match'; 
        } else if (roll < 0.35) { 
            if(hasSent) currentMode = 'cloze'; else currentMode = 'std';
        } else if (roll < 0.60) { 
            currentMode = 'rev'; 
        } else { 
            currentMode = 'std'; 
        }
        
        if (currentMode === 'match') prepareMatchMode(); else renderStandardMode();
        preloadSheet();
    }, 200);
}

function prepareMatchMode() {
    let others = currentBookData.filter(i => i.id !== currentWordObj.id); shuffle(others);
    let subset = [currentWordObj, ...others.slice(0, 3)];
    matchPairs = subset.map(item => ({ id: item.id, ar: item.word, cn: item.def_cn }));
    matchedCount = 0;
    const card = document.getElementById('cardContainer');
    let leftItems = [...matchPairs]; shuffle(leftItems);
    let rightItems = [...matchPairs]; shuffle(rightItems);
    let html = `
        <div class="word-header" style="min-height:auto; padding:15px; background:#f9f9f9;">
            <div class="pos-badge">è¿çº¿åŒ¹é…</div><div style="font-size:14px;color:#666;">ç‚¹å‡»å·¦è¾¹ï¼Œå†ç‚¹å³è¾¹è¿›è¡Œè¿æ¥</div>
        </div>
        <div class="match-container" id="matchArea">
            <svg class="match-svg" id="matchSvg"></svg>
            <div class="match-col">${leftItems.map(i => `<div class="match-item ar" onclick="handleMatchClick('left', ${i.id}, this)">${i.ar}</div>`).join('')}</div>
            <div class="match-col">${rightItems.map(i => `<div class="match-item" onclick="handleMatchClick('right', ${i.id}, this)">${i.cn}</div>`).join('')}</div>
        </div>`;
    card.innerHTML = html; selectedLeft = null; selectedRight = null; document.getElementById('btnShow').style.display = 'none';
}

function handleMatchClick(side, id, el) {
    if (el.classList.contains('matched')) return;
    document.querySelectorAll(`.match-col:nth-child(${side==='left'?2:3}) .match-item`).forEach(d => d.classList.remove('selected'));
    el.classList.add('selected');
    if (side === 'left') selectedLeft = { id, el }; else selectedRight = { id, el };

    if (selectedLeft && selectedRight) {
        if (selectedLeft.id === selectedRight.id) {
            drawConnection(selectedLeft.el, selectedRight.el, true);
            selectedLeft.el.classList.add('matched'); selectedLeft.el.classList.remove('selected');
            selectedRight.el.classList.add('matched'); selectedRight.el.classList.remove('selected');
            const item = matchPairs.find(p => p.id === selectedLeft.id); speakText(item.ar);
            selectedLeft = null; selectedRight = null; matchedCount++;
            if (matchedCount === 4) { score += pointsPerWord; document.getElementById('score-text').innerText = "å¾—åˆ†: " + Math.round(score); setTimeout(() => { alert("ğŸ‰ å®Œç¾åŒ¹é…ï¼"); nextWord(); }, 500); }
        } else {
            drawConnection(selectedLeft.el, selectedRight.el, false);
            setTimeout(() => { selectedLeft.el.classList.remove('selected'); selectedRight.el.classList.remove('selected'); selectedLeft = null; selectedRight = null; }, 500);
        }
    }
}
function drawConnection(el1, el2, isCorrect) {
    const svg = document.getElementById('matchSvg'); const rect1 = el1.getBoundingClientRect(); const rect2 = el2.getBoundingClientRect(); const containerRect = document.getElementById('matchArea').getBoundingClientRect();
    const x1 = rect1.right - containerRect.left - 5; const y1 = rect1.top + rect1.height/2 - containerRect.top; const x2 = rect2.left - containerRect.left + 5; const y2 = rect2.top + rect2.height/2 - containerRect.top;
    const line = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'line');
    line.setAttribute('x1', x1); line.setAttribute('y1', y1); line.setAttribute('x2', x2); line.setAttribute('y2', y2); line.setAttribute('stroke', isCorrect ? '#4CAF50' : '#F44336');
    svg.appendChild(line); if (!isCorrect) setTimeout(() => line.remove(), 500);
}

function renderStandardMode() {
    const card = document.getElementById('cardContainer'); card.innerHTML = `<div id="standardModeContent"><div class="word-header" id="question-header"></div><div class="options-area" id="options-container"></div></div>`;
    const header = document.getElementById('question-header'); const optContainer = document.getElementById('options-container'); const spkClass = canSpeak ? 'audio-icon' : 'audio-icon disabled';

    if (currentMode === 'std') {
        header.innerHTML = `<div class="pos-badge">${currentWordObj.pos}</div><div class="ar-word">${currentWordObj.word}</div><div style="color:#888;font-family:monospace;">${currentWordObj.ipa}</div><div class="${spkClass}" onclick="speakText('${currentWordObj.word}')">ğŸ”Š</div>`;
        createOptions(true);
    } else if (currentMode === 'rev') {
        header.innerHTML = `<div class="pos-badge">${currentWordObj.pos}</div><div style="font-size:24px;font-weight:bold;color:#333;margin:10px 0;">${currentWordObj.def_cn}</div><div style="color:#999;font-size:14px;">è¯·é€‰æ‹©å¯¹åº”çš„é˜¿è¯­å•è¯</div>`;
        createOptions(false);
    } else if (currentMode === 'cloze') {
        let sent = currentWordObj.sent_ar; const regex = createFuzzyRegex(currentWordObj.word); let isReplaced = false;
        const safeSent = sent.replace(regex, () => { isReplaced = true; return '<span class="cloze-gap">_____</span>'; });
        const finalSent = isReplaced ? safeSent : sent + ' <br><span class="cloze-gap">_____</span>';
        header.innerHTML = `<div class="pos-badge">æ‹¼å†™å¡«ç©º</div><div class="sentence-cloze">${finalSent}</div><div style="font-size:15px;color:#555;margin-top:10px;font-weight:bold;">${currentWordObj.def_cn}</div><div style="font-size:12px;color:#999;">è¯·åœ¨ä¸‹æ–¹è¾“å…¥é˜¿è¯­å•è¯ (æ— éœ€æ ‡ç¬¦)</div>`;
        optContainer.innerHTML = `<div class="cloze-input-container"><input type="text" id="clozeInput" class="cloze-input" placeholder="åœ¨æ­¤è¾“å…¥..." autocomplete="off"><button class="cloze-submit-btn" onclick="checkCloze()">æäº¤ç­”æ¡ˆ</button></div>`;
        setTimeout(() => document.getElementById('clozeInput').focus(), 100);
    }
}

function createOptions(isChineseOpts) {
    const container = document.getElementById('options-container'); let options = [];
    if (isChineseOpts) {
        let distractors = currentBookData.filter(i => i.id !== currentWordObj.id).map(i => i.def_cn); shuffle(distractors); options = distractors.slice(0, 3).map(txt => ({ txt, isCorrect: false })); options.push({ txt: currentWordObj.def_cn, isCorrect: true });
    } else {
        let distractors = currentBookData.filter(i => i.id !== currentWordObj.id).map(i => i.word); shuffle(distractors); options = distractors.slice(0, 3).map(txt => ({ txt, isCorrect: false })); options.push({ txt: currentWordObj.word, isCorrect: true });
    }
    shuffle(options);
    options.forEach(opt => { const btn = document.createElement('button'); btn.className = 'option-btn' + (!isChineseOpts ? ' ar-opt' : ''); btn.innerText = opt.txt; btn.onclick = () => checkOption(btn, opt.isCorrect); container.appendChild(btn); });
}

function checkOption(btn, isCorrect) {
    if (isAnswered) return; isAnswered = true; const correctTxt = currentMode === 'std' ? currentWordObj.def_cn : currentWordObj.word;
    if (isCorrect) { btn.classList.add('correct'); score += pointsPerWord; document.getElementById('score-text').innerText = "å¾—åˆ†: " + Math.round(score); speakText(currentWordObj.word); }
    else { btn.classList.add('wrong'); document.querySelectorAll('.option-btn').forEach(b => { if (b.innerText === correctTxt) b.classList.add('correct'); }); setTimeout(openSheet, 600); }
}

function checkCloze() {
    if (isAnswered) return; const input = document.getElementById('clozeInput'); const userVal = input.value.trim(); if(!userVal) return; isAnswered = true;
    const normalizedUser = stripTashkeel(userVal); const normalizedTarget = stripTashkeel(currentWordObj.word);
    if (normalizedUser === normalizedTarget) { input.style.borderColor = "#4CAF50"; input.style.backgroundColor = "#E8F5E9"; input.value += " âœ…"; score += pointsPerWord; document.getElementById('score-text').innerText = "å¾—åˆ†: " + Math.round(score); speakText(currentWordObj.word); document.querySelectorAll('.cloze-gap').forEach(g => { g.innerText = currentWordObj.word; g.classList.add('revealed'); g.style.color = '#4CAF50'; }); }
    else { input.style.borderColor = "#F44336"; input.style.backgroundColor = "#FFEBEE"; document.querySelectorAll('.cloze-gap').forEach(g => { g.innerText = currentWordObj.word; g.classList.add('revealed'); }); setTimeout(openSheet, 800); }
}

function nextWord() { if (currentIndex < currentBookData.length - 1) { currentIndex++; loadCard(currentIndex); } else { alert("ğŸ‰ è¯¾ç¨‹ç»“æŸï¼æœ€ç»ˆå¾—åˆ†: " + Math.round(score)); goHome(); } }
function speakText(text) { if(!canSpeak) return; try { const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text); u.lang = 'ar-SA'; u.rate = 0.9; window.speechSynthesis.speak(u); } catch(e){} }
function preloadSheet() { document.getElementById('sheet-word').innerText = currentWordObj.word; document.getElementById('sheet-ipa').innerText = currentWordObj.ipa; document.getElementById('sheet-def-cn').innerText = currentWordObj.def_cn; document.getElementById('sheet-def-ar').innerText = currentWordObj.def_ar || ''; const setBox = (id, ar, cn) => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if(!ar && !cn) el.style.display='none'; else { el.style.display='block'; el.querySelector('.detail-ar').innerText = ar || ''; el.querySelectorAll('div')[2].innerText = cn || ''; }}; setBox('sheet-collo-box', currentWordObj.collo_ar, currentWordObj.collo_cn); setBox('sheet-sent-box', currentWordObj.sent_ar, currentWordObj.sent_cn); }
function openSheet(){document.querySelector('.modal-overlay').classList.add('show');document.getElementById('detail-sheet').classList.add('show');}
function closeSheet(){document.querySelector('.modal-overlay').classList.remove('show');document.getElementById('detail-sheet').classList.remove('show');}
</script></body></html>
